## NEW_YORK.TLC_YELLOW_TRIPS_2009
mta_tax: FLOAT | $0.50 MTA tax that is automatically triggered based on the metered rate in use
fare_amount: FLOAT | The time-and-distance fare calculated by the meter
dropoff_datetime: NUMBER | The date and time when the meter was disengaged.
tolls_amount: FLOAT | Total amount of all tolls paid in trip.
total_amount: FLOAT | The total amount charged to passengers. Does not include cash tips
pickup_latitude: FLOAT | Latitude where the meter was engaged
imp_surcharge: FLOAT | $0.30 improvement surcharge assessed trips at the flag drop. The improvement surcharge began being levied in 2015.
passenger_count: NUMBER | The number of passengers in the vehicle. This is a driver-entered value.
payment_type: TEXT | A numeric code signifying how the passenger paid for the trip. 1= Credit card 2= Cash 3= No charge 4= Dispute 5= Unknown 6= Voided trip
trip_distance: FLOAT | The elapsed trip distance in miles reported by the taximeter.
extra: FLOAT | Miscellaneous extras and surcharges. Currently, this only includes the $0.50 and $1 rush hour and overnight charges.
rate_code: NUMBER | The final rate code in effect at the end of the trip. 1= Standard rate 2=JFK 3=Newark 4=Nassau or Westchester 5=Negotiated fare 6=Group ride
tip_amount: FLOAT | Tip amount – This field is automatically populated for credit card tips. Cash tips are not included.
pickup_longitude: FLOAT | Longitude where the meter was engaged.
pickup_datetime: NUMBER | The date and time when the meter was engaged.
dropoff_latitude: FLOAT | Latitude where the meter was disengaged
store_and_fwd_flag: TEXT | This flag indicates whether the trip record was held in vehicle memory before sending to the vendor, aka “store and forward,” because the vehicle did not have a connection to the server. Y= store and forward trip N= not a store and forward trip
dropoff_longitude: FLOAT | Longitude where the meter was disengaged.
vendor_id: TEXT | A code indicating the TPEP provider that provided the record. 1= Creative Mobile Technologies, LLC; 2= VeriFone Inc

## NEW_YORK.TREE_CENSUS_2015
boro_ct: NUMBER | This is the boro_ct identifyer for the census tract that the tree point falls into.
st_assem: NUMBER | State Assembly District in which tree point is located
health: TEXT | Indicates the user's perception of tree health.
boroname: TEXT | Name of borough in which tree point is located
problems: TEXT | NULL
root_other: TEXT | Indicates the presence of other root problems
st_senate: NUMBER | State Senate District in which tree point is located
borocode: NUMBER | Code for borough in which tree point is located
y_sp: FLOAT | Y coordinate, in state plane. Units are feet
longitude: FLOAT | Longitude of point, in decimal degrees
nta_name: TEXT | This is the NTA name corresponding to the neighborhood tabulation area from the 2010 US Census that the tree point falls into.
trunk_wire: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a trunk problem caused by wires or rope wrapped around the trunk
tree_id: NUMBER | Unique identification number for each tree point
x_sp: FLOAT | X coordinate, in state plane. Units are feet.
stump_diam: NUMBER | Diameter of stump measured through the center, rounded to the nearest inch.
block_id: NUMBER | Identifier linking each tree to the block in the blockface table/shapefile that it is mapped on.
state: TEXT | All features given value 'New York'
brch_other: TEXT | Indicates the presence of other branch problems
zip_city: TEXT | City as derived from zipcode. This is often (but not always) the same as borough.
cb_num: NUMBER | Community board in which tree point is located
cncldist: NUMBER | Council district in which tree point is located
user_type: TEXT | This field describes the category of user who collected this tree point's data.
trnk_light: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a trunk problem caused by lighting installed on the tree
address: TEXT | Nearest estimated address to tree
spc_common: TEXT | Common name for species, e.g. "red maple"
zipcode: NUMBER | Five-digit zipcode in which tree is located
root_grate: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a root problem caused by metal grates in tree bed
brch_shoe: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a branch problem caused by sneakers in the branches
nta: TEXT | This is the NTA Code corresponding to the neighborhood tabulation area from the 2010 US Census that the tree point falls into.
spc_latin: TEXT | Scientific name for species, e.g. "Acer rubrum"
status: TEXT | Indicates whether the tree is alive, standing dead, or a stump.
steward: TEXT | Indicates the number of unique signs of stewardship observed for this tree. Not recorded for stumps or dead trees.
guards: TEXT | Indicates whether a guard is present, and if the user felt it was a helpful or harmful guard. Not recorded for dead trees and stumps
root_stone: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a root problem caused by paving stones in tree bed
sidewalk: TEXT | Indicates whether one of the sidewalk flags immediately adjacent to the tree was damaged, cracked, or lifted. Not recorded for dead trees and stumps.
created_at: DATE | The date tree points were collected in the census software
curb_loc: TEXT | Location of tree bed in relationship to the curb; trees are either along the curb (OnCurb) or offset from the curb (OffsetFromCurb)
latitude: FLOAT | Latitude of point, in decimal degrees
trnk_other: TEXT | Indicates the presence of other trunk problems
brch_light: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a branch problem caused by lights (usually string lights) or wires in the branches
tree_dbh: NUMBER | Diameter of the tree, measured at approximately 54" / 137cm above the ground.

vert_other: TEXT | Other Vertical Treatment Present
status: TEXT | Excellent: full, well balanced crown and limb structure; leaves normal size color; no dead or broken branches; trunk solid; bark intact. Good: crown uneven or misshapen; some mechanical damage to bark or trunk; some signs of insects or disease; leaves somewhat below normal size and quantity; some dead or broken branches (less than half of the tree). Poor: large dead limbs with over one- half of the tree already dead or removed; large cavities; drastic deformities; leaves significantly below normal size and quantity; severe insect or disease damage. Dead: dead tree; leaves absent; twigs brittle. Shaft: all branches removed; trunk left standing; sprouts may or may not be evident. Stump: stump shorter than breast height; leaves entirely absent or present only on stump sprouts Empty pit: Pit contains exposed soil and no tree

B = Summation of 2 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
C = Summation of 3 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
D = Summation of 4 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
E = 1 report of 12-hour precipitation amount
F = Summation of 2 reports of 12-hour precipitation amount
G = 1 report of 24-hour precipitation amount
H = Station reported '0' as the amount for the day (eg, from 6-hour reports), but also reported at least one occurrence of precipitation in hourly observations--this could indicate a trace occurred, but should be considered as incomplete data for the day.
I = Station did not report any precip data for the day and did not report any occurrences of precipitation in its hourly observations--it's still possible that precip occurred but was not reported

B = Summation of 2 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
C = Summation of 3 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
D = Summation of 4 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
E = 1 report of 12-hour precipitation amount
F = Summation of 2 reports of 12-hour precipitation amount
G = 1 report of 24-hour precipitation amount
H = Station reported '0' as the amount for the day (eg, from 6-hour reports), but also reported at least one occurrence of precipitation in hourly observations--this could indicate a trace occurred, but should be considered as incomplete data for the day.
I = Station did not report any precip data for the day and did not report any occurrences of precipitation in its hourly observations--it's still possible that precip occurred but was not reported
